Subchromosome

Basic stats

Here are some basic statistics about the genome coverage.

  • BOC (breadth of coverage: the proportion (in %s) of the genome covered by at least one read.): 98.69
  • CV (the coefficient of variation.): 2.57
  • DOC (the sequencing depth (Depth of Coverage), that is the average the genome coverage.): 5.02
  • MAD (median of the absolute median deviation defined as median(|X-median(X)|).): 1.44
  • Median (Median of the coverage.): 4.76
  • STD (standard deviation.): 12.90

Regions Of Interest (ROI)

The following tables give regions of interest detected by sequana. Here are the definitions of the columns:

  • mean_cov: the average of coverage
  • mean_rm: the average of running median
  • mean_zscore: the average of zscore
  • max_zscore: the higher zscore contains in the region
